  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_7d399b6f-9ccd-464e-8c9d-e8c1556a9567'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

It was not the first time my father had been in prison and it wouldn't be the last. The Silver Demon's MC was a notorious group of criminals who lived by the code of the road and gave modern society and all it entailed a great big f**k you.<br /><br />"Never forget the day Eva came bouncin' into my f**ked up life, shakin' pigtails, singin' Janis, wearin’ chucks and sharin' peanuts and straight up stole any decency I had left which wasn't a whole lot but she f**kin' took it and I've been hers ever since."</span>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/1064648-i-m-fourteen-and-i-love-romantic-books">I&#39;m fourteen and I LOVE romantic books. The problem is I&#39;m starting to feel like they&#39;re all the same story in various different shades. Is this book worth it?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_1064648'><a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F16109563-undeniable">like</a></span>

</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionTimestamp'>
<a href="/questions/1064648-i-m-fourteen-and-i-love-romantic-books">3 years ago</a>
</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionPermalink'>
<a href="/questions/1064648-i-m-fourteen-and-i-love-romantic-books">See all 2 answers</a>
</li>
</ul>
</div>

</div>
<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/77580316-mason-hawk"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1582842343i/77580316._UX100_CR0,30,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/77580316-mason-hawk">Mason Hawk</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">This is a harsh story about people who don't make what is viewed as 'the right' life choices and pay a high price for doing so. There are many 'Trigge<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">This is a harsh story about people who don't make what is viewed as 'the right' life choices and pay a high price for doing so. There are many 'Trigger' scenes that even have adults upset. It's about a life that only 1% live and should not be viewed as remotely common place. It's a sad convoluted couple that I would not use the word "romantic" to describe. Last, I don't know a 14 year old that I think should read this. I don't even know a 21 year old I would recommend it to. It's not like the adults keeping something good from you, more like this is something you'll wonder why even adults read. Remember 13% of adults found it an unpleasant read...<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_441155896" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/441155896" />
    <a title="P.A. Lupton" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5889210-p-a-lupton"><img alt="P.A. Lupton" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442600938p2/5889210.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/441155896?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P.A. Lupton" class="user" itemprop="url" name="P.A. Lupton" href="/user/show/5889210-p-a-lupton">P.A. Lupton</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781301741724" href="/book/show/16082535-undeniable">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5889210-p-a-lupton?shelf=erotica-i-want-to-read">erotica-i-want-to-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer441155896" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1933627009012648885"><br/>Well, I can’t say I wasn’t warned. I feel like I’m missing something. I scroll through the reviews and look at all the 5 star ratings and wonder if I read the same book. I can kind of see why people rate this book 5 star. It’s extremely emotional and sucks you into the story, there is a ton of conflict, and Deuce is the poster boy for bad boys. And we all know how women like their bad boys. But sadly, for me, it was too much. <br/><br/>You ever watch Jerry Springer? I’ve watched it, and I’m usually sittin</span>
  <span id="freeText1933627009012648885" style="display:none"><br />Well, I can’t say I wasn’t warned. I feel like I’m missing something. I scroll through the reviews and look at all the 5 star ratings and wonder if I read the same book. I can kind of see why people rate this book 5 star. It’s extremely emotional and sucks you into the story, there is a ton of conflict, and Deuce is the poster boy for bad boys. And we all know how women like their bad boys. But sadly, for me, it was too much. <br /><br />You ever watch Jerry Springer? I’ve watched it, and I’m usually sitting there wondering why people love the show so much. You have these crazy losers (sorry, not really nice but true) up on stage, screaming at each other because one person slept with another person who has a baby with absolutely no idea who the father is. Well, add drugs, extreme violence, rape and organized crime to the mix and you have Undeniable. I’ve never <i>ever</i> had the urge to delve into the lives of the crazy, screwed up people who frequent Jerry’s show, so I don’t know why I did it now.<br /> <br />I think most people who read this story will either give it a 1 star rating or a 5 star rating, I doubt there will be much in between. It’s definitely a love or hate book. I was well on my way to a 5 star and then it all went to hell. <br /><br />So, why did I give the book 1 star? <br /><br /><b>Eva.</b><br /><br />I absolutely do not like Eva as a heroine. I like to connect with a heroine, and I definitely have to agree with at least some of their decisions. Well, to me Eva is one of the stupidest women I’ve ever read about. I actually do feel sorry for her being raised in the environment she was raised in. It’s disgusting that she grew up around drug dealing, whores and infidelity and then grows up and wants to raise her kids in the same exact environment. And I’m supposed to think that’s a sweet and happy epilogue? Not only do I dislike her for being a terrible mother, but I was so pissed at her when she gets raped by her almost-brother and then not only forgives him, but tells him she loves him and marries him. Huh? Who the hell does that? On top of that, she has no self-esteem. She walks in on Deuce multiple times while he’s having sex with another woman and she forgives him—forgives him and allows it to continue. I wonder if she realizes she’s a door mat. I guess though, she deserves it since she started sleeping with him while he’s <i>married</i>. It’s just not possible for me to connect with a woman like this, and why would I want to. And for the life of me, I can't figure out why all the men love her.<br /><br />It's not just Eva, though. None of the characters in this book have a single redeeming quality between them. I am glad about one thing, though. I’m glad Deuce and Eva ended up together. They <i>deserve</i> each other. I’m sure they’ll live miserably ever after, raising the next generation of immoral, screwed up children.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13117749241734075533"><b>3.5 stars (I rounded up to four stars). <i>A tangled web of crazy.</i></b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/media/FUN/MEN-AND-MEN-WOMEN/Bildschirmfoto2012-10-10um234617.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"There it is, darlin'," he said softly, his lips curving slowly in a sexy grin. "Nothin' like seein' a pretty girl gettin' all fired up."<br/>I. Just. Stared.<br/>"Back of a bike is comin' for ya and soon too, cuz baby, the way you're lookin' at me is tellin' me you want it. And you want it bad."</i>
</b><br/><br/>First of all let me apologize to you all because I wanted to write a very short review but I just. Can't. Do. It.<br/><br/>Granted, curiosity got the be</span>
  <span id="freeText13117749241734075533" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars (I rounded up to four stars). <i>A tangled web of crazy.</i></b><br><br><a href="http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/media/FUN/MEN-AND-MEN-WOMEN/Bildschirmfoto2012-10-10um234617.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396153i/763384._SY540_.png" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>"There it is, darlin'," he said softly, his lips curving slowly in a sexy grin. "Nothin' like seein' a pretty girl gettin' all fired up."<br>I. Just. Stared.<br>"Back of a bike is comin' for ya and soon too, cuz baby, the way you're lookin' at me is tellin' me you want it. And you want it bad."</i>
</b><br><br>First of all let me apologize to you all because I wanted to write a very short review but I just. Can't. Do. It.<br><br>Granted, curiosity got the better of me AND I was feeling kind of adventurous. That's the reason I wanted to read <i>Undeniable</i> in the first place. Additionally, I thought <i>"Why not reading something a little bit out of my comfort zone?"</i> I'm talking about the cheating. That's usually not my cuppa.<br><br>Ms. Sheehan applied the term f@ck/f@cked/f@cking <b>505</b> times, so please bear with me because I'm going to use this lovely term rather often in my review of <i>Undeniable.</i> As a matter of fact, I think it's justified to stoop to a certain level now and then. Furthermore, I would like to encourage potential readers of <i>Undeniable</i> to read my spoilers. As far as I can judge it's very wise to be well-prepared before diving into this mess. Let's get started…<br><br><br>Dear Deuce,<br><br>Did you know that many readers said that <i>Undeniable</i> is similar to KA's <i>Motorcycle Man?</i> Would you like me to show you a nice visual? <br><br><b>KA's MM</b><br><br><a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/miscellaneous/?action=view&amp;current=large_Pussy_Cat_Photos_28549.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396153i/763385.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Madeline Sheehan's Undeniable</b><br><br><a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/miscellaneous/?action=view&amp;current=dog-attack-on-elderly-749507.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396153i/763386.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Er…the cheating…I hope you remember how many times you cheated on your queen of hearts. What did you just say, Deuce? You can't remember anymore? Did I get that right? Dude, that's not good…I'd suggest this:<br><br><a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/miscellaneous/?action=view&amp;current=Bildschirmfoto2012-11-01um223502.png" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396153i/763387.png" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Get a grip, man! Go squat in a corner, you deserve it. Shame on you! Bad, bad Deuce. *nods head vigorously* You don't need to flex your muscles coz I'm not afraid of you. <br><br>I have to tell you that I find it quite amazing who had sex with whom, how many times they did the deed <b>without</b> catching an STD. Condoms, anyone? I suppose tough biker dudes and bitches are immune to Aids and other STDs. *cough* But the old ladies are not immune at getting pregnant. <br><br><a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/gifs/?action=view&amp;current=htckd5jpg-1.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/405587.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yup. Boom. <br><br><b>The KA factor</b><br><i>A little example:</i><br><br>"(…)You are too good and too sweet and a man like Chase didn't deserve a taste of that kind of beautiful!"<br><br>Does this sound familiar to you, Deuce? The more I read the more familiar sounded anything and everything of <i>Undeniable. </i> The voice and writing is very, <b>very</b> KA. As it is, the <b>only big difference is the violence and the fact that every character is pretty much f@cked up.</b> While KA's asshole-<i>ish</i> heroes have redeeming qualities, I can hardly see that happening in <i>Undeniable.</i> I'm sorry, Deuce, but I tell it as I see it. Hence, the truth hurts now and then.<br><br>Dude, I swear I knew what I had to expect when I started to read <i>Undeniable.</i> So, I'd say this whole mess didn't come as a shock. Then again, I really had to put all of my shortcomings and beliefs far away to be able to actually like your story. I'll be honest, I didn't enjoy it, I didn't love it either but I liked it quite a bit and I loved the ending. Wow, I loved to see your vulnerable and softer side. Additionally, there is something very positive about this story: an older, very hot and sexy man in his fifties. <b>
  <i>You.</i>
</b> I'm a sucker for attractive older heroes. I know, I'm guilty as sin when I say that I want to see more of those older and very yummy heroes. *sigh* After going back and forth I rounded up to four stars because your story is an <b>enthralling as well as intriguing read.</b> It's raw, gritty and disturbing. Hence, it's a dark look at a lifestyle that is incredibly far away from <b>my</b> (cushioned) mainstream life. <br><br>Deuce, please read this paragraph:<br><br><i>I was not going to cry. Nope. Just because he wasn't the man I'd thought he was didn't mean I was going to cry. It was my own fault, putting him on some kind of pedestal when in reality he was just another biker, who lies, cheats, and steals and who can't resist slutty club ass.</i><br><br>Yup, I'm feelin' you, dude, you're pretty speechless right now, aren't you? Nope, do not defend yourself! I gave you something to think about and let's leave it at that.<br><br>One thing's for sure, our equal opportunities officer would have a field day with your story. Women are basically treated like s@it. There's an excessive amount of crudity, foul language, cheating, <b>degradation of women,</b> violence etc. And there is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[rape. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Hey, calm down, Deuce! It's true and there's no need to throw a fit.<br><br>I'm honest when I say that I have my issues with certain characters, however, first and foremost I have issues with your queen of hearts. Eva is an odd one. She is <b>hysterical</b> to no end (screaming, more screaming, lots of screaming, slapping, punching…you get the gist), kinda weak and needy. Yes, please, tell Eva to reel it in! In case you didn't know it yet, this book is filled with plenty of hysterical women…just saying. Oh, before I forget it, your story is filled with plenty of men who can't keep their dicks in their pants either. Don't know what's worse, hysterical women or uber horny badass biker guys. Whatever. *shrugs*<br><br>And then I can't for the life of me understand why Eva would say to the overbearing, crazy as f@ck, homicidal Frankie that she loved him after <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[being raped by the very same man. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Did you know that, Deuce? Imagine, instead of giving him the boot, she spent years with this sicko. Yikes! You have to be seriously f@cked up to do that. Yup, I really get it, this is another lifestyle, it's gang life, it's about committing crimes, and it's ugly, gritty and dark. That said, I completely understand that someone who grew up with this lifestyle may think and act differently because their options are limited. But still…<br><br><i>There are three different types of men in this world. There are weak men; men who run and hide when life slaps them in the ass. Then there are men; men who have a backbone yet occasionally, when life slaps them in the ass, will rely on others. And then there are real men; men who don't cry or complain, who don't just have a backbone, they are the backbone. Men who make their own decisions and live with the consequences, who accept responsibility for their actions or words. Men who, when life slaps them in the ass, slap back and move on. Men who live hard and die even harder.</i><br><br>Now, let's talk about <i>you</i> being an a@@hole. Did you actually growl at me right now? Back off, you jerk!<br><br>When I hit the 83 % mark I was a hair's breadth away from smashing my Kindle against a wall. You said to Eva:<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ "You heard me, bitch. I wish I never f@ckin' touched you. Never f@ckin' met you. You've done nothin' but f@ck with my life."  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>Clue in, you a@@hole, that's exactly what you did with her life as well. Oh, excuse me, both of you did the very same. Oh, please, stop whining! That's pathetic. *shakes head*<br><br>Well, imagine it got worse at 85 % when ZZ told you <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">["Eva!" He said breathlessly. "She's not talkin'…eyes are closed…so much f@ckin' blood…called an ambulance…" Do you remember, Deuce? Poor Eva went into premature labor and almost died thanks to you. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Yeah, you moron did a mighty fine job. Sorry, I'm being sarcastic.<br><br>You treated Eva like s@it, left her alone because you had to f@ck other whores (yes, I got it you are NOT a one-woman man). However, you knew that she was not only <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[pregnant coz it was a high-risk pregnancy but on top of that, you didn't look after her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> You couldn't do it since you were too busy to sort your s@it by f@cking other women's brains out. Simply put, you completely forgot how much she meant to you. Do f@cking right by her and man the f@ck up! Poor Deuce. *pets*<br><br>But then you justified your bad behavior by telling yourself that you couldn't afford to go soft, to get weak and Eva made you so weak and soft. Duh? You thought when you were spending too much time with her you'd end up gluing her to your side. Uh-huh. Again, clue in, you a@@hole, that's called love. Ever heard of that before? There are "things" happening in this story that made me think time and again <i>"Some people are so slow on the uptake."</i> Sheesh. You said you needed space and a clear head but what do you do, huh? Scary Deuce got s@itfaced. *pulls hair* <br><br><i>She gave a shaky laugh that made his chest ache. He'd f@cking hurt his woman real bad.</i><br><br>Ah, I see, a chastened hero; better late than never! *pets some more*<br><br>My biggest issue was the fact that even though you and Eva ended up together, you could not. Keep. Your. Dick. In. Your. Pants. It was disappointing as well as frustrating. Yes, I know, I have to deal with it.<br><br><a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/gifs/?action=view&amp;current=lH3Wb.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396153ra/763388.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ultimately that brought you to your knees:<br><br><i>There wasn't a name powerful enough to describe what he was feeling, to convey what was happening inside of him. It was beyond words, surpassed all emotions. It was living death.</i><br><br>In conclusion, <i>Undeniable</i> is a recommended read <b>if</b> you are able to handle f@cked up characters, a crazy story, excessive cheating and swearing, violence and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[rape. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>If you can't cope with it, then you will end up like this:<br><br><a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/gifs/?action=view&amp;current=wpnT5.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396153ra/763389.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Deuce, fair warning, if you don't treat Eva like a queen, then I'll be back and you won't be enjoying what I'm going to do to you:<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <br>
  <a href="http://s1071.photobucket.com/albums/u520/MsBaba4/FUN/?action=view&amp;current=image.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396153i/763390._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <br>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Take care and all the best,<br><br>Baba<br><br><br><br><b>As a side note</b><br>There are lots of errors (i.e. missing words, incorrect use of words, spelling errors). The book needs <b>major</b> editing/proofreading. <br><br><br><i>
  <b>"What about your dream?"<br>His face went dimples. "I'm lookin' at it, darlin'."</b>
</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer453314143" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14012082152435375125"><br/><b>DISGUSTING,NASTY,REPULSIVE,ABOMINABLE,REVOLTING and .....I LOVE it!</b><br/><br/>Readers be prepared for one hell of a ride.<br/><br/><b>WARNING-Please be prepared for the worst because it's nearly impossible to get off once started!!But feel free to scream,rant,rave,....all you want.</b><br/><br/><i><br/>PROLOGUE--<br/><br/>Mark Twain said,"The two most important days in your life is the day you were born and the day you find out why."<br/>I don't remember the day I was born but I remember the day I found out why.<br/>His name was Deuce.<br/>He was my "why".<br/>And this </i></span>
  <span id="freeText14012082152435375125" style="display:none"><br /><b>DISGUSTING,NASTY,REPULSIVE,ABOMINABLE,REVOLTING and .....I LOVE it!</b><br /><br />Readers be prepared for one hell of a ride.<br /><br /><b>WARNING-Please be prepared for the worst because it's nearly impossible to get off once started!!But feel free to scream,rant,rave,....all you want.</b><br /><br /><i><br />PROLOGUE--<br /><br />Mark Twain said,"The two most important days in your life is the day you were born and the day you find out why."<br />I don't remember the day I was born but I remember the day I found out why.<br />His name was Deuce.<br />He was my "why".<br />And this is our story.<br />It is not a pretty one.<br />Someparts of it are downright ugly.<br />But it's ours.<br />And because I believe everything happens for a reason,I wouldn't change a thing.</i><br /><br /><b>She</b> is the daughter of Damon Fox, aka 'Preacher',who is the president of the Silver Demon MC (motor-cycle club).She was practically raised by all of the gang members,spoilt a lot and of course can wrap them around her little fingers.<br /><br /><b>He</b> is the son of the earlier president of Hell's Horseman MC,and now himself is the president.<br /><br />They are rival gangs.None of them will hesitate putting the other to ground.A momentary truce exists between them now.<br /><br /><b>He is Deuce and she is Eva.<br /><br />This is <u>their</u> love story.<br /><br />Just not a romantic,flowery or dreamy one.<br /><br />This is a hard,bitter and raw one.</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>First meeting--</i>
</b><br /><br />Eva is five.Her father is in prison.She has come with uncle Joe to visit him.They tell her to go and grab a snack.<br /><br />And there,by the snack machines,shaking her butt and singing Summertime way out of tune,she meets <b>him.</b><br /><br />Deuce is twenty-three.He’s visiting his father too.The only difference,he hates his father.He has never known any kindness and love,until he meets <b>her.</b><br /><br /><b>And thus their journey began.</b><br /><br />Filled with pain, betrayal, sorrow, lust, jealousy, hypocrisy,..... <br /><br />And <b>LOVE!!</b><br /><br /><br />They meet again and again and again.....<br /><br />They love again and again and again......<br /><br />They lose each other again and again and again......<br /><br /><b>It’s FATE which pushes them together.It’s LOVE which binds them together and it’s HATE,LUST,BETRAYAL... which tears them apart.</b><br /><br /><i>"I was not going to cry. Nope. Just because he wasn't the man I'd thought he was didn't mean I was going to cry. It was my own fault, putting him on some kind of pedestal when in reality he was just another biker, who lies, cheats, and steals and who can't resist slutty club ass."</i><br /><br />Yes,she has always put Deuce up in a pedestal and loved him.<br /><br />But can she love the real man? <b>The man who gives a whole new dimension to the word ‘asshole’?</b><br /><br /><i>"Son, you are a fuckin’ moron. You wanna know what I see? I see a girl who isn’t just a girl but a fuckin’ prize and why the fuck she chose an asshole like you to give that fuckin’ prize to I haven’t a fuckin’ clue. Stupid if you ask me."</i><br /><br />Can Deuce realize this?Can he redeem himself once and for all?Or will it be too late?<br /><br />There are other people who want to tear them apart.<br /><br /><b>Chase-</b> Husband of Eva's best friend Kami.This manipulative sick bastard loves Eva.He wants her.And is ready to use every tactic to get Eva.<br /><br /><b>Frankie-</b> He too loves Eva.Obsessively.Possessively.If he can't get her,no one else can.<br /><br />The author has very cleverly put these two people with their own definitions of love next to Deuce.<br /><br />As a reader,I was forced to ask-<b>What is love??<br />Is it what Chase and Frankie feel for Eva?What kind of love is so cruel?Love is never cruel.Then how is their love different from Deuce's love?He too cheats ,lies and hurts Eva.</b><br /><br /><i>"There wasn't a name powerful enough to describe what he was feeling, to convey what was happening inside of him. It was beyond words, surpassed all emotions. It was living death."</i>--Deuce when he saw Eva getting raped by Frankie,unable to help.<br /><br />This is where all my questions were answered.<br /><br /><br /><b>So,readers,I cannot tell any more.For this is <u>their</u> story to tell.Yes some parts are downright ugly,some are insane...and you'll have to ride through these.But the end is beautiful.That,I assure you.</b><br /><br /><br /><i>EPILOGUE</i><br /><br /><b>He closed his eyes.</b><br /><br /><i>He stuck out his hand.<br />Name's Deuce sweetheart. My old man here is Reaper. It was nice talkin' with ya."<br />She put her tiny hand in his and he squeezed.<br />"Eva," she whispered. "That's my name and it was so, so great to meet you too."<br />He smiled.<br />She smiled.</i> <br /><br /><b>The rest is fuckin' history.</b><br /><br /><br /><br />---The End---<br />(Please remember that it is strictly for above 18.)</span>

<div id="review_440895324" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/440895324" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/440895324?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781301741724" href="/book/show/16082535-undeniable">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to ~ Becs ~ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/2673922-zusi">Zusi</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=biker-hero">biker-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=gamma-hero">gamma-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer440895324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13806451314192691681"><b>Oh. My. God</b><br/><br/>What the <b>HELL</b> did I just read??<br/><br/>This was compelling, emotionally exhausting and yet strangely uplifting – this book is mad, it’s all kinds of wrong and yet, oh my God, I just totally <b>DEVOURED</b> it! It grabbed me by the throat right at the beginning, dragged me through the story barely allowing me to breathe and threw me in a heap at the end twitching, barely lifeless. This book <b>OWNED</b> me and it really shouldn’t have. The heroes are <b>JERKS</b>, the women don’t behave much better and yet I was c</span>
  <span id="freeText13806451314192691681" style="display:none"><b>Oh. My. God</b><br /><br />What the <b>HELL</b> did I just read??<br /><br />This was compelling, emotionally exhausting and yet strangely uplifting – this book is mad, it’s all kinds of wrong and yet, oh my God, I just totally <b>DEVOURED</b> it! It grabbed me by the throat right at the beginning, dragged me through the story barely allowing me to breathe and threw me in a heap at the end twitching, barely lifeless. This book <b>OWNED</b> me and it really shouldn’t have. The heroes are <b>JERKS</b>, the women don’t behave much better and yet I was compelled to keep reading, I lost sleep, I didn’t care – I just had to finish it!!<br /><br />So, this is the story of Eva and Deuce and, unusually for contemporary romance, their story spans several decades. They first meet when Eva is 5 and Deuce is 23, both visiting their fathers in prison. Eva’s father is the president of an MC and Deuce is about to inherit that role of a rival MC when his father dies. Right from the getgo, Eva is in love with Deuce and she has caught his eye. They meet sporadically over the years until Eva is 16, Deuce, 34 and they become intimate and he eventually takes her virginity at 18 – I mentioned the wrongness right?<br /><br />This is set in the badass world of Motorcycle Clubs and it’s raw, rough, edgy to say the very least as the story absolutely hurtles along like a runaway train out of control. It practically pulsates with an energy, a lifeforce of its own. Deuce behaves like a jerk to Eva for nearly all the book but true love is undeniable and, despite everything that goes down and boy does it go down, their feelings for one another completely outweigh time and everything that happens.<br /><br />Deuce is such a badass and he is a jerk with a big old capital J – I hated the way he treated women, the way he spoke to them but yet still I <b>LOVED</b> him – what the heck is wrong with me? I’ve decided that Madeline Sheehan has managed to lace the pages with some kind of twisted magic that sucks you in, reaches in through your chest, grabs your heart and squeezes tight and doesn’t let go. This book also contains quite a few things that are normally like red flags to me when I'm reading, infidelity to name just one, but the compulsion to carry on with the story completely overcame my normal, set in stone, hang-ups.<br /><br />I’m making it sound bad and it certainly is very rough round the edges but it’s taut, it’s raw, it’s edgy and it’s incredibly compelling and despite muttering things like ‘He did not just do that’ ‘ No way he just said that to her’, I was fascinated and could not put the damned book down. Underneath the mass of thorns that is the way everyone behaves in this book, there is this beautiful rose blooming and that is the love between Eva and Deuce – it’s a constant throughout the book although you may have to look hard to see it sometimes.<br /><br />I will say that the editing was not up to par in this book – the typos jumped out at me thick and fast in the first half of the book. They may well have been there in the second half of the book too but, by that point, I was reading so fast I didn’t notice, nor did I actually care!<br /><br />I’m going to highly recommend this one – it’s slightly reminiscent of Kristen Ashley’s Motorcycle Man but much rougher around the edges and far less rose-tinted.<br /><br />4 badass stars<br /><br />Thanks to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/2673922-zusi" rel="nofollow noopener">Zusi</a> for the most awesome rec!<br /><br /><i>
  <i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Blog</a></i>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13806451314192691681" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_442049041" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/442049041" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/442049041?book_show_action=true">Oct 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Stacia (the 2010 club) by: </span>
      Buddy read w/Rebecca and Amanda 
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=frustrating">frustrating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=drama-llama">drama-llama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=romantica-or-erotica">romantica-or-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer442049041" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer302914038716810181"><b>Update 11/29/12</b> Rating dropped for reasons I'm no longer allowed to say due to GR rule changes. My original review for the book stands in order to comply with GR policy.<br/><br/><br/><b>Original 3 star review from 10/25/12</b><br/><br/>Header removed because photobucket is not worth my time anymore. It pretty much said something about me trying to be objective.<br/><br/>I promised that if I read <i>Undeniable</i>, I would be fair and objective as per dictionary.com's definition (adj.) : <i>not influenced by personal feelings, interpretations, or</i></span>
  <span id="freeText302914038716810181" style="display:none"><b>Update 11/29/12</b> Rating dropped for reasons I'm no longer allowed to say due to GR rule changes. My original review for the book stands in order to comply with GR policy.<br /><br /><br /><b>Original 3 star review from 10/25/12</b><br /><br />Header removed because photobucket is not worth my time anymore. It pretty much said something about me trying to be objective.<br /><br />I promised that if I read <i>Undeniable</i>, I would be fair and objective as per dictionary.com's definition (adj.) : <i>not influenced by personal feelings, interpretations, or prejudice</i>. Yes, I had a bit of a bias going into this book. Part of me still feels shady about even reading the book, since I wouldn't have done it if <i>Undeniable</i> hadn't been compared to <i>Sons of Anarchy</i> (my favorite t.v. show). But I did cave and read the book, and I now I will give my thoughts.<br /><br /><b>Warning :</b> There will be some mention of the graphic level of content in this book. I have written a fairly spoiler-free review in terms of plot, but have mentioned certain things that happen in the book which I think people might want to know about before picking it up so they can decide if they want to even read this (such as the mention of rape scenes).<br /><br />I can easily predict that if this book makes it big, there are two things which will happen in true <i>Twilight, Fifty Shades of Grey, and Beautiful Disaster</i> style :<br /><br />1. People will go crazy about the book, name it as one of their favorites, and recommend it to everyone they know.<br />2. People will pick up the book, think it's the biggest piece of sexist, abusive crap, and will write scathing reviews.<br /><br /><b>So where do I stand?</b> I'm right there in the middle. Because I understand that you can't profile a certain type of lifestyle without showing the gritty underlying truth, I wasn't personally offended by the fact that real-life issues came up in the story such as rape, cheating, degrading of women by calling names, etc. When you're dealing with club life, gang life, crime life, etc. etc. <i>people aren't going to react the way someone living in mainstream society necessarily would.</i> Children are born into a lifestyle, they are raised in it, and they grow up to continue the lifestyle, not always taught that they have other/better options. It's easy to sit back from the outside and scream at the female that she's being idiotic for allowing herself to be used and abused, but we're looking at it from a place of knowing that there are other options.<br /><br />I have the feeling that <i>Undeniable</i> will be hard for some people who might not find it easy to separate out their world view from someone else's world view. I also have the feeling that there might be people who will fully understand the concept of what is going on and could still rate this book low because some of the content isn't something <i>that they'd want to read about</i>. It's probably safer not to read the book if you know the content won't be your thing, but I don't get to make that decision for anyone else.<br /><br />For pure story readability, this was an engaging book. It was gritty, dark, violent, sexy, and disturbing. If this were a movie or t.v. show, I'd love every second of it. Not once was I bored. Even when things were happening that I didn't like, I was still fully into what was going on.<br /><br />As a cohesive book, my thoughts are mixed. There were errors everywhere. Never have I seen such apostrophe abuse - I'm not sure why so many words which needed to be made plural had apostrophes added to them. I also saw incorrect uses of words such as your and you're, as well as plenty of spelling errors. <br /><br />The excessive amount of swearing and crudeness didn't bother me given the subject matter, but I sort of sighed at how much of the book read like Kristen Ashley dialogue. I don't think there was any sort of copying or anything like that because I completely get that men who live a rougher style are going to speak in a more stilted manner...it was just too close for my comfort level at times.<br /><br /><b>Final thoughts :</b> Entertaining story that went a little bat-shit crazy at times. I think a few things went round and round to the point where they were beaten to death <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Deuce still being a jerkwad after they got together frustrated me in a way that it didn't when he was doing it beforehand <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. If my copy had some editing and a few areas reigned in at times, I might have gone slightly higher on the rating because <i>Undeniable</i> had me sucked into its web. <br /><br />I'd recommend this to people who can handle controversial subject matter and like it when true bad boys (read : assholes) are reformed. If you're looking for ultra-alpha males and lots of crazy, sexy time, you'll find it with this book. And if you're a SoA fan, just picture Deuce as Jax (hey, he had the shoulder length blonde hair!) and you'll enjoy it that much more. :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="302914038716810181" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_439508975" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/439508975" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/439508975?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781301741724" href="/book/show/16082535-undeniable">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer439508975" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5238245453037351015"><b>5 FAN-F*CKIN-TASTIC STARS</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Name's Deuce sweetheart. My old man here is Reaper. It was nice talkin' with ya."<br/>She put her tiny hand in his and he squeezed.<br/>"Eva," she whispered. "That's my name and it was so, so great to meet you too."<br/>He smiled.<br/>She smiled. <br/>The rest is f*ckin' history.</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>WOW, WOW, WOW!!!!</b> This book...<b>OH.MY.GOD</b> words fail me. Okay, so here I go trying to actually put into words my dying love for Eva and Deuce. When I first read the synopsis for this book I was honestly thinking What </span>
  <span id="freeText5238245453037351015" style="display:none"><b>5 FAN-F*CKIN-TASTIC STARS</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Name's Deuce sweetheart. My old man here is Reaper. It was nice talkin' with ya."<br />She put her tiny hand in his and he squeezed.<br />"Eva," she whispered. "That's my name and it was so, so great to meet you too."<br />He smiled.<br />She smiled. <br />The rest is f*ckin' history.</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>WOW, WOW, WOW!!!!</b> This book...<b>OH.MY.GOD</b> words fail me. Okay, so here I go trying to actually put into words my dying love for Eva and Deuce. When I first read the synopsis for this book I was honestly thinking What The F*ck? I mean in all honesty the synopsis is awful but I love it when a book comes with a warning sign because then I feel the need to pick it up immediately. Yes, I know that makes me twisted but twisted, dark and sinful books call to me. This books message rang clear as a bell for me <b>TRUE LOVE</b> (well a f#$%ed up insane version of true love...lol) , the theme that I love in my books. I am a hopeless romantic and am drawn to messed up love stories because I always believe in the theory that love can conquer all. Deuce and Eva's love can definitely conquer all! The challenges they face are <b>HUGE, EXTREME</b> but they love each other and with that their journey begins.<br /><br />Deuce meets Eva when she is 5 years old and he is 23. Eva is on her way to see her daddy "Preacher" who is serving a 5 yr sentence on Rikers island. Eva is the sweetest kid around, she's friendly and when she see's Deuce she immediately takes a liking to him and insist on meeting Deuces dad who is also serving a sentence on Rikers island. Eva leaves a HUGE impression on Deuce and I PROMISE nothing sexual is involved, it's not creepy it's just a chance meeting that leaves an impression on him and 5 year old Eva.<br /><br />They meet again when Eva is 12 and then again when she is 16. At sixteen things heat up a little bit, it's nothing crazy but they do heat up. The real action begins when Eva is 18 and the story that ensues is incredible.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>His lips brushed against my cheek. "If you were older darlin', I'd have you on the back of my bike and in my f*ckin' bed and you'd be not just likin' it but lovin' it, beggin' me for more." ~~ Deuce.</b>
</i><br /><br />Deuce....sigh!! <b>ALPHA MALE</b> at it's best. I have never read an alpha male as hot as him. He turns you to putty in 5 seconds but holy crap can he be a douchebag and an as*hole. I think that's what makes him so delicious. He is possessive and protective and the president of his MC. He has womanizing issues and screws anything with legs but has a soft heart that just makes you want to wrap him up in your arms and devour him. His fierce attraction and love for Eva make him completely swoon-worthy. He is FAR from perfect though and has to learn how to love her the right way.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"Can't f*ckin' live without you. Want you on my bike and in my bed. Want my kid's inside you. Want you by my side babe for as long as I got left." ~~ Deuce</b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="5238245453037351015" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/459091056" />
    <a title="Ada" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11500057-ada"><img alt="Ada" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1391266240p2/11500057.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/459091056?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ada" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ada" href="/user/show/11500057-ada">Ada</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11500057-ada?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11500057-ada?shelf=freakin-amazeballs">freakin-amazeballs</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer459091056" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3582474550170840194">My first review EVAH!!! I have no idea how I should do it, but here goes nothing…<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/656992.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br/><b> "Here's all you have to know about men and women: women are crazy and men are stupid. And the main reason the women are crazy is that men are stupid." (George Carlin) </b><br/>------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br/><br/>I couldn't have said it better myself and if you add crazy love in the </span>
  <span id="freeText3582474550170840194" style="display:none">My first review EVAH!!! I have no idea how I should do it, but here goes nothing…<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/656992.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br><b> "Here's all you have to know about men and women: women are crazy and men are stupid. And the main reason the women are crazy is that men are stupid." (George Carlin) </b><br>------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br><br>I couldn't have said it better myself and if you add crazy love in the mix, you get "Undeniable".<br>Undeniable comes with a warning, then I'm all in. This book is rough, raw, gritty, dark, disturbing, intense, gruff, a total brain and heart haywire and most people say it's not recommended to everybody. I may be mistaken, but I would most definitely recommend this to everyone. Fiction just got real, people! This is how life is (rough, raw, disturbing, intense, etc.), especially life in a Motorcycle Club (I guess).<br><br>I'm still trying to "reel it in" after the shock I got from the first sentence in the book. My facial expression was something like this:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769052.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And throughout the book:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769053.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sweet Jesus mother Mary!!!! I knew I was going to give this a 5 star read in a nanosecond. Let me get this straight?! This book is written by a WOMAN??!! Damn, woman, I think I'm having a major girl crush on you. Please let me take a moment to say: <b> "I LOVE YOU, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6554504.Madeline_Sheehan" title="Madeline Sheehan" rel="nofollow noopener">Madeline Sheehan</a> !!!!!!" </b><br><br>So... lets meet Eva:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398121i/769054._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Born, raised in a MC and constantly surrounded by bickers (lucky bitch :P )<br>And Eva around Deuce:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769055.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And there's Deuce:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398121i/769056._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I'm sorry, words fail me when it comes to him *SWOON*<br>And Deuce every time near Eva (LOL):<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769057.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And here's their story:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769058.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Hahahaha... well, not quite. There's a lot of <b> crazy </b>, fuckwads bickers, bitches and whores, old men and old ladies, and one spoiled brat, Kami, Eva's bestie, and Kami's husband, Chase.<br>This book was out of sunshine and rainbows, but damn me if I didn't laugh my ass off. The way the bickers talk to each other, the dialogue between Deuce and Eva and I'm personally in love with Cox and Ripper. I have never read the F word so many times in a single book, but goddammit I loved every billionth time I read it. F**k hearts and flowers, I wanna be a bicker chick or a bicker's chick (defo the last one).<br>Did I mention this book is full of CRAZY?! Enter, Frankie:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769059.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I might be the same kind of crazy as he is, cause I loved him, too. ( I loved all the characters, all were so well written)<br>And more crazy... Hell's Horsemen + Silver Demon's + Deuce + Preacher = <b> BATSHIT CRAZY </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769060.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Undeniable was a breath of fresh air after so many billionaires and super-model men and the eternal falling in love in 3 days. It kind of was what happened to Deuce and Eva, but not really. Do I make any sense? No?! Then you need to read it. I have so many wonderful, amazing words to say about this outstanding book, but I don't want to ruin it. Here's when I fell hopelessly in love with Deuce and I think I will again and again, because I'm going to read this book till every fuckin' word is imprinted in my not-so-sane brain:<br><br>Deuce: "You respect women you little fuckin' shit. It was a fuckin' woman who carried you around in her fuckin' body, fuckin' birthed you and fuckin' loved you, and it's gonna be a woman who keeps you warm at night, who lets you inside her body and it's gonna be a woman who carries around your fuckin' children. You fuckin' respect that, you feel me? You fuckin' respect women, all of ‘em, or I will end you." <br><br>And my favorite part: Deuce - "Gonna make some boy happier than a pig in shit." ( a true poet, LMFAO)<br><br>ONE OF THE BEST BOOKS OUT THERE and it should be a MUST READ NOW and a MUST READ AGAIN AND AGAIN!!!!!!!! Madeline Sheehan, you freakin' rock<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769061.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Best fucked up love story and I loved it<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769062.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3582474550170840194" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5136145129717427438"><b>.99cents TODAY 5/23/13 LINK: ttp://<a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.com/B009N539DS'>amzn.com/B009N539DS</a><br/>This Review contains Minor Spoilers-none will hinder your reading experience.<br/></b>-This review is for person 18 yrs and older. Reader discretion is advised.<br/>5 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre: Adult Romance<br/><b><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16082535.Undeniable__Undeniable___1_' title='Undeniable (Undeniable, #1) by Madeline Sheehan' rel='nofollow noopener'>Undeniable</a> had characters that came at me like a<i> SHARK attacking it's prey undetected.</i> Cunning Raw and Untouchable. <br/><br/>This is not your average love story.....</b><br/>Eva met the love of her life at the age of five. He was twenty-three.<br/>She is the daughter of a MC Presid</span>
  <span id="freeText5136145129717427438" style="display:none"><b>.99cents TODAY 5/23/13 LINK: ttp://<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.com/B009N539DS">amzn.com/B009N539DS</a><br />This Review contains Minor Spoilers-none will hinder your reading experience.<br /></b>-This review is for person 18 yrs and older. Reader discretion is advised.<br />5 STARS out of 5<br />Genre: Adult Romance<br /><b><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16082535.Undeniable__Undeniable___1_" title="Undeniable (Undeniable, #1) by Madeline Sheehan" rel="nofollow noopener">Undeniable</a> had characters that came at me like a<i> SHARK attacking it's prey undetected.</i> Cunning Raw and Untouchable. <br /><br />This is not your average love story.....</b><br />Eva met the love of her life at the age of five. He was twenty-three.<br />She is the daughter of a MC President. He is the son of a MC president.<br />She is a Silver Demon. He is a Hell's Horseman.<br /> No, this is not a paranormal book .<br />MC stands for motorcycle club. Silver Demon and Hell's Horseman are the names of two rival gangs of criminals who go by their on set of rules.<br /><i><br />You and me kid, we were fuckin’ born in the life, reared by the road and the wheel; it’s what we know and where we belong but that don’t mean it won’t take its toll. So you promise me, no matter what you see, no matter what sort of fucked up shit happens to you. Don’t let this life turn you bitter.”</i><br />~Deuce to Eva<br /><br /><b>Deuce and Eva</b><br />Eva meets the love of her life in a common yet unexpected place on the right day at the right time. FATE. They both have a connection it is in no way, shape or form sexual. It was more like kindred spirits connecting. Through out her life the years pass and they have run in's with one another. <br />When she is sixteen he no longer sees the skinny little girl she once was. He sees a girl becoming a woman. When Eva is eighteen he desires the woman he sees, he wants the woman he sees, he takes the woman that he sees.<br /><i><br />'He saw the change in me, noticed it instantly. His nostrils flared and his eyes darkened with hunger. I knew this look. Deuce was hungry. I was food. I loved that look. It made me feel beautiful, powerful and utterly feminine. I sucked in air through my nose willing myself to stay put when I wanted nothing more than to run to him, strip him naked and fuck him blind.</i><br />~Eva's Inner Monologue<br /><br />Nothing about their journey is easy, it is filled with<b> pain, pleasure, lust betrayal, death, and unforeseen consequences.</b> Some good, some bad.<br />In the end all they have is <b>LOVE.</b><br /><i>
  <b><br />He filled with primal male satisfaction. She wanted him. Her, a fucking angel in a mess of demons, wanted him, one of the biggest fucking demons he knew.</b>
</i> ~Deuce <br /><u><br />Thoughts</u><br />I loved this book! It was ALPHA MALE HEAVEN! The author kept me on the edge of my seat the whole time. It was everything I needed and wanted in a book. It was raw, intense, edgy and emotional. I could tell the author was unafraid to take risk with her characters and push their limits. As a reader I LOVED that. I found the characters to be very well developed, we felt their emotions and understood their actions. Whether we liked them or not. I fell in love with a lot of the secondary characters too especially Cox and Kami.<br /><br />CHARACTERS<br /><b>Eva-</b> I loved Eva even though I did not always agree with her decisions. She was fun fearless and played a dominant role in the life of plenty of ALPHA MALES. I loved her. Flaws and all. Period.<br /><b>Kami-</b> Was another character I absolutely loved she is Eva's best friend and was a hilarious ball of fire. Check her out in the scene I posted below<br /><i><br />“Boys?”</i> Kami swept her long blonde hair over her shoulder and cocked her hip. <i> <br />“This is my last summer of freedom. My dad is a rich asshole who is making me marry another rich asshole. I have three months left before I become a proper little Jackie O and have to start fucking my staff just so I can get off. That being said, if you guys don’t mind sharing, I’ve got a whole lot to give.” </i> <i><br />“I don’t,”</i> Cox said quickly.<i><br />“Nope, me either,”</i> Ripper said.<br /><b><br />The Men<br />Deuce-</b> RAW. All masculine all alpha no in between. If you are with him, what he says goes. Period. He was DELICIOUS I fell head over heels in love with his character. He messed up and I forgave him every damn time.<b><br />Frankie-</b> UNTOUCHABLE. I coined him untouchable because the guy reminded me of a lion roaming the jungle like he owned it, knowing that no one would dare touch him. Eva could though.... He loved Eva and he was obsessive and possessive with her. She was like his anchor, she could tame his beast. Or could she???<br /><b>Chase-</b> CUNNING. The guy was manipulative. He was patient and knew when to strike to get what he wanted. He was also an asshole. BIG TIME.<br />I hated and empathized for both him and Frankie. Bravo to the author for bringing out those feelings in me.<br /><br /><u>Fave Lines said and unsaid</u> <i><br />My mouth loved Deuce, my hands loved Deuce, my body loved Deuce. Loved, loved, loved, loved… I loved Deuce. Loved.</i> ~Eva's Inner monologue<br /><i><br />"Know I don't deserve nothin' as sweet as you,"</i> He whispered darkly as his hand dipped in between my legs. <i><br />"Anything a man's gotta steal to have he don't deserve."</i> <i><br />“You didn't steal this,”</i> I breathed, writhing against his hand. <i><br /> "I gave it."</i> ~Deuce and Eva<br /><i><br />"My cash is legally earned,"</i> Chase stated.<i> "Not a drop of blood on it."</i> I glared at him. <i> <br /> "You're a lawyer Chase. There's blood all over you." </i> ~Chase and Eva<br /><i><br />"There you fuckin' are Eva. Gotta keep fuckin' you to remind you where you belong, I got no problem with it."</i> ~Deuce<br /><i><br />“Son, you are a fuckin’ moron. You wanna know what I see? I see a girl who isn’t just a girl but a fuckin’ prize and why the fuck she chose an asshole like you to give that fuckin’ prize to I haven’t a fuckin’ clue. Stupid if you ask me.</i> ~Blue to Deuce, referring to Eva<br /><br />My Ratings<br />Characters- I loved some I hated some<br />Writing Style- Excellent<br />Plot/Storyline- Suspenseful, Sexy, Raw and Intense<br />Steam Factor- High/Very Steamy<br />Overall- I loved it!!! Read it!<b><br /><br /> Now go forth and read then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br /><br /><b> WARNING</b>- This story spans over twenty years. The hero and the heroine <br /> both have relations with other people. If you do not like your hero and heroine to be with other people than this book is NOT FOR YOU. This book also has two rape scenes though they are not graphic. If you cannot handle rape scenes then this book is NOT FOR YOU.<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16082535.Undeniable__Undeniable___1_" title="Undeniable (Undeniable, #1) by Madeline Sheehan" rel="nofollow noopener">Undeniable</a></span>

    <u>crash and burn</u>
  </i>
</b>.....it was one helluva of a ride and I don't ever want to be on it again and I want to experience it one more time...and one more time...and one more time....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397468ra/766961.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Was there anything that the author left out?......lemme see....this book has criminals, psychopaths, rapists, cheaters, more criminals, murderers, liars, manipulative jerks, prostitutes, criminals, and then some jealousy, envy, hatred, enmity, lust, lies, betrayals, craziness, obsession, addiction, and twisted, crazy LOVE.<br><br>The first rape scene I came across I was like <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379780581i/408020.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">.....<br>I couldn't believe what I was reading....how can a person who claims to love her so much do that?....but in <b>a strange, perverted way it made perfect sense</b>...how can a person who is <b>sooooo obsessed</b> with her that if another man even looks at her goes crazy <b>
  <i>not</i>
</b> hurt her?....he is bound to....<br><br>Then if I hated it so much what was it that made me go on? It was <b>moments like these</b>: <br><br><i>They'd spent only moments together. Here and there, some good, most painful. It didn't make any sense. They didn't make any sense. He should have let her go a long time ago. But he couldn't.  And he still couldn't. Because he didn't want to. Because he fucking loved her.</i><br><br><b>Eva knew what a jerk he was</b>....had seen his assholiness....but for her he was <i>"The most beautiful man I’d ever seen and still the biggest asshole I'd ever met. And I loved him still. That had never changed."</i><br><br>Her feelings for him kinda reminded me of Adele's <b>'Set Fire To The Rain'</b>.<br><i>I let it fall, my heart<br>And as it fell, you rose to claim it<br>It was dark and I was over<br>Until you kissed my lips and you saved me<br><br>My hands, they're strong<br>But my knees were far too weak<br>To stand in your arms<br>Without falling to your feet<br><br>But there's a side to you that I never knew, never knew<br>All the things you'd say, they were never true, never true<br>And the games you play, you would always win, always win<br><br>But I set fire to the rain<br>Watched it pour as I touched your face<br>Let it burn while I cry<br>'Cause I heard it screaming out your name, your name.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397468i/766962.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Deuce to Eva:</b> <i>"Fuckin' listen Eva and listen good. Words are shit and I ain't good with them anyway. So here’s the fuckin’ truth for you, straight up, I'm forty eight years old, gonna be forty nine all too soon and I damn well know a good thing when I see it and babe all I’ve ever been able to fuckin' see is you. <b>Not many chances a man has in his lifetime to do right, to earn the love of a good woman, and to get a taste of true freedom. And babe, for me, you're all fuckin' three.</b> Have been for a good while now. Whatever this shit is between us it’s always been there and it’s always gonna be there.  I’m shit-fuckin’-tired tryin’ to ignore it. I’ll try to do right by you Eva, you’d be the first, but I’ll fuckin’ try my damndest. <b>And baby, true freedom is the open road, the wind on your face and a good woman on the back of your bike holdin’ you tight like you’re her reason for breathin’ because she sure as fuck is yours.</b>”</i><br><br>But sadly despite his claims that he was no good with words and that he would do right by her he turned out wrong on both counts. <b>Wish it had been the other way round.</b><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397468ra/766963.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Like one wise biker rightly put it:</u>
</b> <i> “Son, you are a fuckin’ moron. You wanna know what I see? I see a girl who isn’t just a girl but a fuckin’ prize and why the fuck she chose an asshole like you to give that fuckin’ prize to I haven’t a fuckin’ clue. Stupid if you ask me. But you’re throwin’ it all away cuz you can’t stop fuckin’ whores and cuz you’re refusing to give her a piece of the club. Not a lot to ask if you ask me but since you ain’t askin’ I’ll shut the fuck up and let you be a fuckin’ moron.”</i> <br><b>This deserves some serious</b><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397468ra/766964.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But these following lines...these made me realize that yes, <b>no matter how much he messed up and screwed up his relationship with her he did love her</b>....what a time to realize it: <br><br><i>He had been beaten within an inch of his life.<br>He had been strangled, stabbed and shot. <br>He had shot, stabbed, strangled, beaten and killed. <br>He'd been hurt, scared, mad, angry as fuck and homicidally inclined. <br>Fuck, he had been so fucking pissed off he'd had his old man killed.  His own flesh and blood. <br>But never, NEVER, had he felt like this.<br>There wasn't a name powerful enough to describe what he was feeling, to convey what was happening inside of him. It was beyond words, surpassed all emotions. <br>It was living death.</i>- when she being raped and he was helpless to save her.<br><br>In the end as in all love stories <b>everyone lived happily ever after....but the whole thing had left me reeling and I haven't been able to find my balance even now</b>...<br><br><i>He stuck out his hand. <br>"Name's Deuce sweetheart. My old man here is Reaper. It was nice talkin' with ya." <br>She put her tiny hand in his and he squeezed. <br>"Eva," She whispered.  "That's my name and it was so, so great to meet you too." <br>He smiled. <br>She smiled.</i> <br><b>The rest is fuckin’ history</b><br><br>God, How <b>I hated reading</b> this book....but fine I admit it I loved it...<b>the messed up love story of two messed up people...I loved it</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397468i/766965.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>P.S.: The <b>1 missing star</b> is for the fact that this <b>isn't the kind of story that I want to read about...it isn't the kind of story which leaves you feeling happy and contended....it isn't the kind to make you go dreamy....but you'll love and hate it anyway</b>.....not the author's fault......and it is strictly for people who can take the <b>raw, crude, mean, vulgar</b> side of life unabashedly and all the nitty gritties that comes with it.<br><br>I still feel like saying <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397468ra/766966.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="2088968975592171483" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
