<div id="review_461792681" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/461792681" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/461792681?book_show_action=true">Nov 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer461792681" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12097042546552760978"><br/><blockquote>
  <b>THIS STORY WAS CRAZY, MESSED UP AND A LITTLE</b>
</blockquote><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398525ra/770353.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><blockquote>
  <b>BUT I LOVED EVERY MINUTE OF IT!!! (well, almost every minute...)</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Undeniable</i>
</b> is one hell of a ride that, at times, left me shocked, repulsed, enthralled and fascinated all at once. It was both really beautiful and extremely ugly and raw at the same time. At times I loved it, other times I hated it. All I can say is that the story managed to grasp my attention from the very first page until the very last one... It left me speechless and I </span>
  <span id="freeText12097042546552760978" style="display:none"><br><blockquote>
  <b>THIS STORY WAS CRAZY, MESSED UP AND A LITTLE</b>
</blockquote><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398525ra/770353.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><blockquote>
  <b>BUT I LOVED EVERY MINUTE OF IT!!! (well, almost every minute...)</b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>
  <i>Undeniable</i>
</b> is one hell of a ride that, at times, left me shocked, repulsed, enthralled and fascinated all at once. It was both really beautiful and extremely ugly and raw at the same time. At times I loved it, other times I hated it. All I can say is that the story managed to grasp my attention from the very first page until the very last one... It left me speechless and I don't think I will ever forget it, EVER. <br><br><b>
  <i>Undeniable</i>
</b> is the story of Eva and Deuce, it's not a pretty story, nor is it a happy one but it is THEIR story and to Eva and Deuce that is ALL that matters.<br><br><i>
  <b>It didn't happen overnight, and it wasn't easy.<br>Nothing worth doing ever is.<br>And love is worth everything.</b>
</i><br><br><u>
  <b>Prologue</b>
</u><br><br><blockquote>
<i>Mark Twain said,"The two most important days in your life is the day you were born and the day you find out why."<br>I don't remember the day I was born, but I remember the day I found out why.<br>His name was Deuce.<br>He was my "why."<br>And this is our story.<br>It is not a pretty one.<br>Some parts of it are downright ugly.<br>But it's ours.<br>And because I believe everything happens for a reason, I wouldn't change a thing."</i><br>~ Eva</blockquote><br><br><u>
  <b>The Story</b>
</u><br><br>When Eva and Deuce first meet; she is five years old, he's twenty three. She's the sweet innocent princess of her father's infamous motorcycle club the Silver Demons, he's the sexy bad ass biker of their rival motorcycle club the Hell's Horsemen. <br><br>They meet by coincidence while they're both visiting their fathers in the same prison. It was faith that brought them together but as Angel Flonis Hareta said: <i>"There will always be a reason why you meet people. Either you need them to change your life or you're the one that will change theirs."</i><br><br>Eva and Deuce did change each others lives, for better or for worse. From the moment they first meet, Eva was already enchanted by the "charming" biker boy.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Deuce got to his feet grinning and gave me a two-finger salute. "Bye, darlin'."<br>Darlin'.<br>It was official. I was head over heels in love.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Deuce, himself was impressed with the little girl too, impressed by her innocence and sweetness and he never managed to get her out of his head ever since...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Never forget the day she came bouncin' into my fucked-up life, shakin' pigtails, singin' Janis, wearin' Chucks, sharin' peanuts, and straight up stole any decency I had left - which wasn't a whole lot - but she fuckin' took it, and I've been hers ever since."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>After that first meeting they don't see each other for several years, but when they meet each other again, the instant connection between them is back. And the fire that sparks between them lights up more and more each time they meet.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>There it is, darlin'," he said softly, his lips curving slowly in a sexy grin. "Nothin' like seein' a pretty girl gettin' all fired up. Back of the bike is comin' for ya and soon, too. 'Cause, baby, the way you're lookin' at me is tellin' me you want it. And you want it bad."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Their encounters are filled with love and passion but every single time there is a reason for their meetings to be accompanied by hurt, hatred and betrayal. Not only do other people try to tear them apart, sometimes they tear each other apart as well... Eva learns that Deuce isn't as perfect as she always imagined him to be. Even when they finally can be together, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Deuce manages to screw up by cheating on her with random women just because he doesn't seem to know any better. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Those scenes made me really mad and I kept thinking: <i>"Why the hell is he so stupid?? If he does that one more time..."</i><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/518394.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p>Yes, parts of the story really enraged me. And if you're going to read it be prepared for some ugliness...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"How could a man be so perfect for me and yet so wrong for me all at the same time?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I often wondered myself that same question about the two of them while reading this story... But in the end they really did love each other and somehow, as crazy as their love for each other was, it all made perfect sense for them to be together...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Hey," I said softly and cupped his cheeck.<br>"Yeah?"<br>"What about your dream?"<br>His face went dimples. "I'm lookin' at it, darlin"."<br>Oh. Crap. My heart felt near bursting. I was absolutely done for. This man owned me, body and soul, and everything in between.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398525i/770354.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"And baby, true freedom is the open road, the wind on your face, and a good woman on the back of your bike, holdin' you tight like you're her reason for breathin', because she sure as fuck is yours."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398525i/770355.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>___________________________________________<br><br><br>Granted, this story was so messed up sometimes, it made me mad and frustrated as hell; but in the end I really loved reading about this crazy-ass couple and their unconditional love for each other... Thinking about everything they've been through and how they still managed to end up the way they did, even brings a tear to my eyes...<br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398525ra/770356.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br>So, for everyone who hasn't read this incredible story yet, I would say: prepare yourself for a CRAZY, WILD ride with a lot of swearing, explicit content and some pretty awful, tear-your-heart-out scenes (that involve cheating and raping). This story might not be for everyone but still, I would advice you to read it and find out for yourself...<br><br>___________________________________________<br><br><br><u>
  <b>Epilogue</b>
</u><br><br><i>"Name's Deuce, sweetheart. My old man here is Reaper. It was nice talkin' with ya."<br>She put her tiny hand in his, and he squeezed.<br>"Eva," she whispered. "That's my name, and it was so, so great to meet you, too."<br>He smiled.<br>She smiled.</i><br><br><b>The rest is fucking history.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398525i/770357.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>****</b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Favorite quotes</b>
</u><br><br><blockquote>
  <b><i>"You and me kid, we were fuckin' born in the life, reared by the road and the wheel; it's what we know and where we belong, but that don't mean it won't take its toll. So, you promise me, no matter what you see, no matter what sort of fucked up shit happens to you, don't let this life turn you bitter."<br><br>**<br><br>"You didn't steel this," I breathed, writhing against his hand. "I gave it." His blue eyes glitterd with amusement. <br><br>"Naïve, darlin'," he murmured. "I stole you a long time ago. Round the time you fuckin' stole me." Fuckin' stole me. He just said that. He really, really, said that. <br><br>"I love you," I breathed into his mouth, overcome by sheer sensation and the larger than life force that was Deuce."</i><br><br>****</b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>4.5 BEAUTIFULLY MESSED UP STARS</b><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br> <br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="12097042546552760978" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

And even though the H/h drove me batty with all their insane drama, I was still captivated and rooting for their HEA.       <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781301741724" href="/book/show/16082535-undeniable">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=explicit">explicit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=must-re-read-again">must-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=cheaters">cheaters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy">lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=first-love-crush">first-love-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=more-than-one-lover">more-than-one-lover</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer439981141" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer146586715811459536">4.75-5 Stars<br/><br/><b>
  <i>Prologue: Mark Twain said, “The two most important days in your life is the day you were born and the day you find out why.”<br/>I don’t remember the day I was born, but I remember the day I found out why.<br/>His name was Deuce.<br/>He was my “why”.<br/>And this is our story.<br/>It is not a pretty one.<br/>Some parts of it are downright ugly.<br/>But it’s ours.<br/>And because I believe everything happens for a reason, I wouldn’t change a thing.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Holy fucking shit. I fucking devoured this book. DE-<i>fucking</i>-VOURED. I'm s</span>
  <span id="freeText146586715811459536" style="display:none">4.75-5 Stars<br><br><b>
  <i>Prologue: Mark Twain said, “The two most important days in your life is the day you were born and the day you find out why.”<br>I don’t remember the day I was born, but I remember the day I found out why.<br>His name was Deuce.<br>He was my “why”.<br>And this is our story.<br>It is not a pretty one.<br>Some parts of it are downright ugly.<br>But it’s ours.<br>And because I believe everything happens for a reason, I wouldn’t change a thing.</i>
</b><br><br>Holy fucking shit. I fucking devoured this book. DE-<i>fucking</i>-VOURED. I'm sorry for my cussing, but this book is 99% swearing, and tack on the fact I already have a sailor mouth, I'm going to be swearing A LOT. There are a million things I want to say, but I have no idea where to start. I’m lost on words. One thing is for sure is that this is not your typical romance. Not. Even. Fucking. Close. It’s raw, gritty and so fucked up, it will give you whiplash. <br><br>**Possible spoilers ahead**<br><br>I have to introduce to you to the main cast of characters. You can get a good feel of the story just by knowing who they are. <br><br><b>Eva Fox</b> – Biker brat and daughter of Preacher. The only one who can control Frankie. First met Deuce when she was only five years old and has been smitten with him ever since.<br><b>Deuce</b> – President of the Hells Horseman motorcycle club. He’s eighteen years older than Eva. Like all bikers, he is sexy as sin, very Alpha and very possessive. Not very faithful to his women, though. <br><b>Frankie</b> - Good looking, pureblooded Italian biker brat who was orphaned when he was only fifteen years old. Preacher took him under his wing when Eva was only twelve. He has a very short fuse, has anger issues and severe abandonment issues. He is prone to night terrors, but finds peace and solace in Eva’s bed (no worries, it remains platonic…at least in the beginning). He is intensely possessive of Eva. He is <b>
  <u>hugely and insanely</u>
</b> jealous of any man coming near her. Will do anything to have her.<br><b>Damon Fox (“Preacher”) </b> – President of the infamous “Silver Demon’s” motorcycle club. He is very protective of his daughter and is one dangerous man. <br><b>Kami</b> - Eva’s BFF. She’s the daughter of a Senator. She is very promiscuous and lived a very wild life prior to her arranged marriage to Chase. Stuck in a loveless marriage, both Chase and Kami agree to engage in multiple affairs. <br><b>Chase Henderson</b> - Highly paid lawyer who graduated from Harvard. Went to prep school with both Kami and Eva. Married to Kami, but has always wanted and loved Eva. Though he is very handsome and smart, he is also a bit of a sleaze and will do whatever it takes to get what he wants.<br><br><b>
  <i>“So I let you treat me like a piece of fucking furniture who’d be right where you left me every time you decided to grace me with your presence because I promised you I wouldn’t run. But I can’t do it anymore!” ~ Eva </i>
</b><br><br>Deuce is Eva’s world. Every small encounter they have is monumental. Just when you think they’ll be together, something always happens to make the other run away. There are tangents all over the place. Multiple lovers, multiple heartaches and just crazy ass, high, intense drama. I’m not really going to go into the plot. There’s just too much going on. Just know that it was no smooth path for Eva and Deuce’s HEA. Far from it. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Get the fuck off her, mother fucker, before I blow a hole through your fuckin’ skull.” ~ Frankie </i>
</b><br><br>My emotions were all over the place in this one. Yes, Deuce and Eva made me crazy, but the character that made me most conflicted is Frankie. If you notice, he’s the one I had to describe the most to. I’m actually disturbed at myself that I felt so much for him. Mentally, he was not all there and to me, he was just an overall sad character. He’s a murderer and just outright psychotic, but the way he died at the end just made me cry. Like Eva, I guiltily had a huge soft spot for him. Yes, call me crazy, but I really couldn’t help it. <br><br>Bikers galore in this book, which means lots of testosterone…a whole lot. With them come the women, the money, the cussing, and the fighting. This book held nothing back. There is rape and violence of every sort in this story, so just be warned. As for me, I’m all about fucked up stories. Yes, yes, we already know I’m disturbed, but I think they’re the best kind. They leave a lasting impression, just like this one. Highly recommend!!<br><br>-----<br><b>
  <u>FOLLOW ME</u>

<span id="freeTextContainer16972472149354435599">I am in the minority here, but....I new the warnings, but nothing prepared me for this...<br/><br/>When I read this book I had difficulties put in to words what I have experienced... but right know I feel the need to voice myself as I am getting more anxious of the progeny of the rapid growing popularity of this gender amongst the readers...   <span id="freeText16972472149354435599" style="display:none">I am in the minority here, but....I new the warnings, but nothing prepared me for this...<br /><br />When I read this book I had difficulties put in to words what I have experienced... but right know I feel the need to voice myself as I am getting more anxious of the progeny of the rapid growing popularity of this gender amongst the readers... I feel social morality is already being questioned and these book are adding more weight towards dissociation... and its becoming more and more of normality.. for example: in the reviews the word "sexy hero" was used repetitively...the hero was 34 when having first sexual encounter with the heroin who was 16 at the time and took her virginity in a full of rats dirty, rotten alley against the wall when she was 18.. IS THAT SEXY? He's all yours.. enjoy it!!! <br /><br />TO THE POINT...<br /><br />The book, is repulsive! It reflects the kind of people with horribly degrading moral compass. So the million dollars question is "WHAT THE WORLD WOULD BE LIKE?? If referring to the people from the book and give them power(For example: people like Hitler and his lack of morals) and allow this patterns of behavior? Let me tell you what... the world would soon end because no way people would stand this shit! Either they would abuse each other, rape each other, cheat on each other, drugged on each other, debased each other and kill each other! because that is precisely how these people interacted to one another in this book! You either hate it or love it, I decided to hate it.<br /><br />I am ok with swearing, but there is a limit that I can take and this is way out of my comfort zone. I understand that many people adored this book which reflects the high rating and I also understand this is that kind of environment that justify the language etcetera... BUT FOR GOD's SAKE DON'T PAINT THIS AS A... WOW WHAT A BEAUTIFUL LOVE STORY, ITS STUNNING...UNIQUE... I AM IN LOVE WITH IT... OK if following this line of thinking...ask yourself a question: is't ok to use infidelity, is't ok to verbally abuse you in front of your child.. Example: Your are f**king bitch/c*nt, is't ok to have sex with your best friend's husband, is't ok to cheat on your women and when she confronts the act, forcing her to see it and sit on the other women's body that your guy is f**ing is't ok to have sex with a women when your girlfriend is pregnant because you need sex and cannot keep your d*ck in your pants, is't ok to abandon your pregnant women to her own fate because you are too busy having sex and when she's 8 month pregnant you are screwing other woman and she caches you on the act but you ignore her and continue the act like nothing happens and then you thrown her like garbage out of the room... And then she is so stressed she and the baby nearly died in a hospital??? As much as how sick that may sound, I wanted Frankie to end up with her and not Deuce because at least Frankie was faithful to her and did not cheated on her and only had eyes on her...right to the very end/ he was sick so its like his choice was taken away from him. And Deuece exactly new what he was doing and continued cheating throughout the entire book so he was just unredeemable character I could not sympathise nor care! But why did she have to kill Frankie???? The guy was in desperate need for some serious psychiatrical help and all these years she could not even provide that for him!!! So she slept with a lawyer to protect him and then killed frankie???? so what's the point protecting him???? But the fact of the matter is the heroin was abused physically and mentally and did't even flinched when walk in on the hero f*** another women because SHE BECAME A PRODUCT OF THIS ENVIRONMENT IN WHICH THIS SORT OF BEHAVIOURS IS NORMAL... and I felt sad for her that she would live like that and bring another child that's life will also be messed up for him. I am also sad to think that majority of reviewers think it sexy! There is no love between the H/h... In normal circumstances it would be a dysfunctional and unhealthy relationship... IS THAT BEAUTIFUL????? GET YOUR FACTS STRAIGHT!!!<br /><br />I AM DONE HERE</span>

You’re going to cry and you’re going to laugh and you’re going to find out how aerodynamic books really are. <br/><br/>And it’s going to be awesome.<br/><br/><b> I promise. </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/e65c3a34d0d4b889670342995f29f354.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422788i/841640._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo e65c3a34d0d4b889670342995f29f354.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/download5.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422788i/841641.jpg' alt=' photo download5.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>Eva meets Deuce when she’s five. Immediately, she’s besotted by the twenty</i></span>
  <span id="freeText5117735805100662784" style="display:none"><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/16109563.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422788i/841639._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 16109563.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>♦ METAL and LEATHER ♦<br>♦ LOYALTY and BETRAYAL ♦ <br>♦ ANGER and SEX ♦<br>♦ WHISKEY and BLOOD. ♦<br>♦ TRIGGER and RELOAD ♦<br><br><b>And one hell of a story.</b><br><br>This <i>isn’t your average love story. It’s gritty and <b>savage</b> and angry and <b>lustful</b>. It’s going to devastate you and it’s going to <b>turn you on</b>. You’re going to cry and you’re going to laugh and you’re going to find out how aerodynamic books really are. <br><br>And it’s going to be awesome.<br><br><b> I promise. </b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/e65c3a34d0d4b889670342995f29f354.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422788i/841640._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo e65c3a34d0d4b889670342995f29f354.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/download5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422788i/841641.jpg" alt=" photo download5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Eva meets Deuce when she’s five. Immediately, she’s besotted by the twenty-three-year-old biker the way all children become besotted by their heroes. Even at five, she’s curious about the tortured sadness in his eyes and how his hands look so rough. Little does she know, that during that same first meeting, he’s completely mystified and dismantled by the little girl and her toothy grins and her loud, boisterous laughter.<br><br>However, during the following years, innocent admiration for each other turns into something else entirely. <br><br>And the story begins…<br><br> <a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/download1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422788i/841642._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo download1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Deuce comes back into town and suddenly the young, gawky Eva is now a more womanly sixteen. And suddenly their relationship becomes a lot more, as the innocence of it becomes nonexistent and admiration sparks into attraction.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/download4-2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422788i/841643._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo download4-2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>After that first exchange, their lives change drastically. Especially because their relationship walks on forbidden territory.<br><br>Eva the daughter of the Silver Demons Motorcycle Club President. <br>And Deuce belongs to their almost nemesis, the Hell’s Horsemen Motorcycle Club.<br><br>But if you think that’ll stop them…<br><br>Think again.<br><br>Over the years; no matter what obstacles tear these two apart, fate always manages to throw them back together<br><br>Because from that very first kiss…<br><br>♦ They developed something <b>inescapable</b> ♦<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422788i/841644.jpg" alt=" photo 2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>And it’s a <b>hell</b> of a ride.<br><br></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="5117735805100662784" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_440079685" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/440079685" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/440079685?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781301741724" href="/book/show/16082535-undeniable">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer440079685" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13276807092077730229">I'm trying to calm down now. It's 2:45am, I just finished the book. I think I may either be in shock, or I'm suffering from PTSD. I don't think I'll be able to fall asleep any time soon. I must review this later... I need to process this. Wow.<br/><br/><b>5 HEART-WRENCHING STARS</b><br/><br/>Where to begin... first of all I want to say that this was a very good book. It was raw and emotional and actually quite disturbing. The story involves the lives of those born into a subculture of society, the MC or Motorcycle club. I</span>
  <span id="freeText13276807092077730229" style="display:none">I'm trying to calm down now. It's 2:45am, I just finished the book. I think I may either be in shock, or I'm suffering from PTSD. I don't think I'll be able to fall asleep any time soon. I must review this later... I need to process this. Wow.<br><br><b>5 HEART-WRENCHING STARS</b><br><br>Where to begin... first of all I want to say that this was a very good book. It was raw and emotional and actually quite disturbing. The story involves the lives of those born into a subculture of society, the MC or Motorcycle club. It is one thing to choose a lifestyle such as this, involving drugs and alcohol, crime rings, and debauchery. Where men are hard and cruel, and women or bitches (appropriately named) are owned, used and passed around like dirty dishtowels. It is another thing altogether to grow up in this world, knowing no other way of life, where your innocence is practically forfeited at birth. This book is glimpse into one life, and what it was like for a young girl born and raised as the child of the MC.<br><br>Eva Fox was 5 years old when she met Cole West. He was twenty-three at the time and known as Deuce to everyone who knew him. Eva was the daughter of Damon Fox, better known as "Preacher," who was the president of the Silver Demon MC and her one and only parent. She was with her Uncle Joe, visiting her father in prison, when she met Deuce. Deuce was 23, and the son of the president of the Horsemen MC. He was there visiting his father, "Reaper" who was also in prison. <br><br>Deuce was immediately taken with Eva. She was so sweet and innocent, boucin' around singing Janice Jopplin tunes to herself, and so open and trusting to him and his father. She took to him instantly, holding his hand, and skipping over to meet his old man. <br><br><b>
  <i>"I am Preacher's little girl. And I'm gonna be just like him when I grow up. I'm gonna have a fatboy but I want mine to be sparkly and I want a pink helmet with skulls on it. And instead of being the club President, I'm gonna be the club Queen cuz I'm gonna marry the biggest, scariest biker in the whole world and he's gonna let me do whatever I want because he's gonna love me like crazy."</i>
</b><br><br>Eva ran into Deuce over the years for only brief moments.. but just enough to know, he was the man of her dreams, or so she had decided. But then there was Frankie. <br><br>Frankie Deluva came to live with Eva and her Dad at the MC, when his Dad, Frankie Deluva, Sr, Preacher's road chief, died in a auto-accident. Frankie was three years older than Eva, and suffered extreme separation anxiety. He had taken to Eva immediately and was extremely protective of her. In fact, he never left her side. As she started to mature, he made it known that she was to be his girl, and wouldn't even allow her to look sideways at another guy. <br><br>Eva had a different plan though... she never forgot about Deuce, and he never forgot about her. Once she hit 16, he was fighting his urges, trying to stay away from her, when he gave in, and crossed the line with her.<br><br><b>
  <i>"If you were older darlin', I'd have you on the back of my bike and in my fuckin' bed and you'd be not just likin' it but lovin' it, beggin' me for more." ..."Back of my bike is comin' for ya and soon too, cuz baby the way you're lookin' at me is tellin' me you want it. And you want it bad."</i>
</b><br><br>Frankie never gave up either. Getting more and more crazy and protective as time went by. But Eva never gave into him. Once Eva finished college, she went gunnin' for Deuce. Little did she know, he was married with kids, livin' in Montana. It didn't stop her though, she still felt they were meant to be together... but things didn't turn out at all like she'd planned. <br><br>Life went on... it wasn't kind to her or to Deuce. Frankie was back in the picture, and getting crazier by the day. I will not elaborate on the details of the drama, but just know that life gets ugly. And it is heart-breaking to watch as Eva loses her innocence and her carefree nature. Hardened by the rough life of the MC, she learns to survive and grow strong.<br><br>I really fell in love with Eva's character from the very beginning. She was a true innocent, who was brought up in the rough life of the MC. She was loved and cherished by her father and his boys, but was still exposed to their hard and amoral world. Where men were often tough and cruel, and women were disrespected, used and discarded like trash. <br><br>I did come to accept many of the characters and their debauchery, but I think I kept wanting to see them grow or redeem themselves in some way. I felt disgusted most of the time, the selfish, indulgent behavior almost reminded me of wild animals instead of people. In fact, I think some species actually treat their females better than these men do theirs. <br><br>Deuce pissed me off incessantly!! I don't think I ever thought he deserved Eva's love. There was this spark of good in him, in the beginning, when he was young. A goodness that I felt was drawn to the goodness in Eva... and I kept waiting for it to re-surface when they finally got together.. but it just never came back. I felt he let her down... and after that, I couldn't find enough goodness in him to forgive. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He did finally come around in the end, but for me.... it was too little too late. I found it hard to accept his feelings as genuine, after he disregarded her for so many years. It shouldn't take two near death experiences and a rape to get your attention!! But he was what she wanted... and she got him. He did finally give her the love and respect she deserved but after so much pain and loss... I just couldn't find it in me to forgive him. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>He did find peace at the end... and she got what she wanted.. but the cost was so high!!! The story became so intense in the end... I could not put the book down!!! It was heart-wretching!!! I felt completely drained by the end. And I have to give high praise to the author for this... what a ride it was. Scary and shocking... and so so sad!!! My heart broke at the end of the book!!! And yes..they finally figured it out, what it was that they wanted, and that they had it with each other.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Whatever this shit is between us its always been there and it's always gonna be there. I'm shit-fuckin'-tired tryin' to ignore it. I'll try to do right by you Eva, you'd be the first, but I'll fuckin' try my damnedest. And baby, true freedom is the open road, the wind on your face and a good woman on the back of your bike holdin' you tight like you're her reason for breathin' because she sure as fuck is yours." </i>
</b> <br>I'm giving this one <b>5 STARS!!!</b> But read with caution.. this story is not for everyone!!!<br><br><b>Eva Fox "Foxy"</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/Olivia-Wilde-actresses-24095937-1968-1996.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380908975i/3176751._SY540_.jpg" alt="Olivia Wilde photo Olivia-Wilde-actresses-24095937-1968-1996.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/OliviaWilde1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_441925326" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/441925326" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/441925326?book_show_action=true">Oct 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer441925326" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5108937827850128125">This was like a Kristen Ashley book on steroids!! It was an orgy of intensities. Intense emotions. Intense sexual encounters. Intense frustration. Intense hatred. Intense...everything! Don't get me wrong, I'm not saying I loved this book. I'm not even sure if I <i>liked</i> this book, but it got under my skin...hard. It was like a patron shot rimmed with crack. It's an addiction entirely self inflicted. A train wreck of desire and want that you can't help but watch! It will strip you bare and leave you</span>
  <span id="freeText5108937827850128125" style="display:none">This was like a Kristen Ashley book on steroids!! It was an orgy of intensities. Intense emotions. Intense sexual encounters. Intense frustration. Intense hatred. Intense...everything! Don't get me wrong, I'm not saying I loved this book. I'm not even sure if I <i>liked</i> this book, but it got under my skin...hard. It was like a patron shot rimmed with crack. It's an addiction entirely self inflicted. A train wreck of desire and want that you can't help but watch! It will strip you bare and leave you raw. Sometimes...it's just about the ride! READ ON!<br /><br /><br /></span>

  <span id="freeText12666040706255573108" style="display:none"><b>OH. MY. GOD. WHAT. A. BOOK.</b><br /><i>HOLY FUCKING HELL! Shit bikers curse more than Pirates &amp; Me combined :P Hehe</i><br /><br />Loved the whole biker world, Seems mad crazy but hell.. it was so interesting, I was stuck to the book like glue.. Stayed up all night and finished it and boy oh so worth it.<br /><br />Seriously, EVA is really motherfuckingly dumb but boy, love at the age of 5.. Thats something ;)<br />Her character was something :D Loved it to bits.. It had its own wicked charm.. A character you could totally fall in love with despite of her craziness.<br /><br />Deuce in my head is this bloody hot biker, Who's bones I'd jump any fucking time :D<br />I really liked him and his foul mouth! He was all hot and *BAM* more hot and sexy and oozing anger!<br />Loved him! Usually older men so aren't me, but boy! Even at 48 he was sexy as fuck!<br /><br />Frankie, Sick lil mother fucker. Seriously, I don't get people and their head issues! Its plain out creepy!!<br />He seriously had some balls of steel!<br /><br />Kami, Crazy bitch, Loved her.. but hell some level of craziness <br /><br />The one lines in the book were amazing! Like plain out crazy and amazing!<br />The amount they've cursed in this book, Hilarious! The author really had her way with the characters, story and her one lines and the cursing!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>His hand was warm and comfortable like my bed was after I'd slept in it all night.</i>
</b> - Awwie<br /> <br /><b>
  <i>"Gonna make some boy happier than a pig in shit." - Deuce</i>
</b> HAHAHAHA, Wtf!!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Fucking skinny bitches everywhere in this city.  No tits.  No ass.  All of them wearing skin tight clothes that emphasized the fact that they had no tits and no ass.</i>
</b> - Hahahahaha! too all the size 0 bitches! 0 isn't a size :P<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Purse?" Joe snorted.  "Dontcha mean that fuckin' potato sack you could fit a family of midgets in?"</i>
</b> Crazy ass bikers!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Preacher snorted.  "Both in our fifties.  Only difference is you got yourself a beautiful, younger woman to keep you young and all I got is a club full of stupid shitheads who think bathing is optional and farting is an art form."</i>
</b> Hahahaha!<br /><br />This book is a must read, You will surely enjoy it to bits!<br />Do write reviews a review, I'd love to read it and cuss like a biker babe while doing so :P</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3493446093140809196"><br/><br/><br/><strong>Holy fuck!!..</strong><br/><br/>Warning:: this is probably more of a rant than a review!!!<br/><br/> MADELINE SHEEHAN, I think I have a girl crush on you!!!! I am a SONS OF ANARCHY junkie. Will admit that because of that show I was eager to read this book. This book though was so intense and captivating that I experienced feelings that I have not felt since I finished The Captive in the Dark Series. <br/><br/> In the beginning I will admit that the age difference at first was a bit disturbing. Then you don't even notice it. You soon </span>
  <span id="freeText3493446093140809196" style="display:none"><br><br><br><strong>Holy fuck!!..</strong><br><br>Warning:: this is probably more of a rant than a review!!!<br><br> MADELINE SHEEHAN, I think I have a girl crush on you!!!! I am a SONS OF ANARCHY junkie. Will admit that because of that show I was eager to read this book. This book though was so intense and captivating that I experienced feelings that I have not felt since I finished The Captive in the Dark Series. <br><br> In the beginning I will admit that the age difference at first was a bit disturbing. Then you don't even notice it. You soon realize though that Eva Fox is an old soul. So you really always feel that she older than she is. Eva, Eva!! I loved her character. She is a bad ass bitch who knows her men well and knows how to handle them better. This story is woven so well that I feel that I personally know Eva and Deuce. That they are in my life and I can't stop grinning. Haven't felt this way since Caleb and Olivia. Not that I was in a slump but diffidently hadn't found my next Caleb and Olivia. I don't know if that is a good thing or bad thing, now I feel empty again because now I miss Deuce and Eva.<br><br> Deuce and Eva's love withstood the test time over and over again. Even once they were truly together they weren't. Yes the writing was vulgar,crude,freaking hot as hell and that is why I believe is what makes their relationship so passionate. They fell in love even before they knew thats what that was. Eva is Deuce's perfect match. Circumstances keep them apart far too long but you never feel bored with the story. It truly is amazing how well written this book is!! I didn't even realize I read 400 pages in such a short time of two days. The story just flowed so well. <br><br><strong>OTHER CHARACTERS THAT MADE THIS BOOK SO GOOD</strong><br><br>FRANKIE<br> I always wanted Deuce and Eva to end up together but I will say that the author made me feel so much for Frankie. Yes he was a sick fuck; but god how I fell for him instantly as well. I cried and cried when the end between them comes. Don't get me wrong the story ended the way it should of; but wow Frankie just stole my heart also. Maybe because he was crazy, maybe because I was hoping he would get help, I don't know why but in the end I loved him.<br><br>KAMI AND COX <br> These two were so engaging that when I was not grinning for Deauce and Eva, I was grinning for Kami and Cox. They were perfect for each other. Kami was also a girl I instantly liked. She never pretended to be anything she wasn't and that was so refreshing. She loved to fuck every which way and she loved to make men want her every which way. She just loved sex!! and she was good at it. So it was a pleasant surprise to see her fall for Cox, yet she never pined for him like a lovestruck girl and I loved that. Their love was hot, rough and just so sexy!!<br><br><br><br><br>I cant wait to read more of Madaline's work!!<br>oo<br><br>My eva<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395499i/761783.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer441577737" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer16413284661279687459"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395462i/761723._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395462i/761724._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Jesus. Fucking. Christ! This book is a whole world of mind fuck. I absolutely loved it.<br/><br/>Warning: Do <i>not</i> read this book if you do not have a completely open mind. It is full of violence, bad language, mindless fucking, whores, murder, rape and every type of corruption you can imagine. But if you like a head-fuck, and want a page turning story, this is gripping. I'm so exhausted from it.<br/><br/>I love the power of the written word... that it can make me fall in love with a bunch of murdering, criminal, dir</span>
  <span id="freeText16413284661279687459" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395462i/761723._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395462i/761724._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jesus. Fucking. Christ! This book is a whole world of mind fuck. I absolutely loved it.<br><br>Warning: Do <i>not</i> read this book if you do not have a completely open mind. It is full of violence, bad language, mindless fucking, whores, murder, rape and every type of corruption you can imagine. But if you like a head-fuck, and want a page turning story, this is gripping. I'm so exhausted from it.<br><br>I love the power of the written word... that it can make me fall in love with a bunch of murdering, criminal, dirty scumbag bikers, that's pretty damn amazing. But it totally did. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I had just hit rock bottom, and I didn't care. In fact, I didn't give a shit about anything at all.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Oh my God, Deuce. Yessss puhlease! So hot. And I don't even know why. He's a complete nut job! He can't keep his dick in his pants, he's got blood on his hands on a regular basis and he is everything a girl should never ever want. But my God, if that doesn't make you want him even more.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Spent too much time married to a bitch I couldn't stand and too much time beatin' myself up for wishin' I was balls feep in a bitch eighteen years younger than me. Add that shit together and that equals me being fuckin' miserable for a long fuckin' time. So yeh, I can't do this anymore. Can't fuckin' live without you. Want you on my bike and in my bed. Want my kids inside you. Want you by my side, babe, for as long as I got left."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Eva. Wow, how is a girl supposed to grow up with any semblance of normality with that upbringing. Yeh, she's not, and she doesn't. She's a fantastic character though. She was hard as nails, feisty, had balls bigger than most men and boobs to match. I loved her, she was great!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You and me, kid, we were fuckin' born in the life, reared by the road and the wheel; it's what we know and where we belong, but that don't mean it won't take its toll. So you promise me, no matter what you see, no matter what sort of fucked up shit happens to you, don't let this life turn you bitter."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I loved the dynamics and the dialogue between all the characters. It sucked me in totally and I read it until I couldn't keep my eyes open and then woke up early to finish it off. It's that kind of book. You get pulled in by every single character, obviously Eva and Deuce... but Preacher, Kami, all the boys, even Frankie. I hated myself for crying to Frankie. It's so fucked up, but I couldn't help it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I hated Frankie. He had fucked me up so badly that I didn't know who the fuck I was.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Still, I have no idea what I just read and what it has done to my brain, not to mention my moral compass. I'm a nice girl... I don't fall in love with mean bikers who kill people and make dirty money. Oh, but, turns out, I do! <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>We got through it. Together. It didn't happen overnight, and it wasn't easy.<br>Nothing worth doing ever is.<br>And love is worth everything.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I have to admit to cheating a little on my casting with this one. I got this image from the <i>Undeniable</i> Facebook group, because there just isn't a better option for Deuce. That's so perfect for him.<br><br>I don't even know what else to write, because this book needs to be read to be understood. But like I said, go into it with an open mind, prepared to be shocked, disgusted and your mind blown. Do that, and you'll love it. Can't handle that heat? Definitely don't even bother picking this up. I loved it! If you like twisted, taboo, mind fuck romance, you will too!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He smiled.<br>She smiled.<br>The rest is fuckin' history.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395462i/761725._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743250626754/?fref=ts">http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743...</a></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny Levine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny Levine" href="/user/show/12673270-jenny-levine">Jenny Levine</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer452605022" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8823300708387895687"><b> <i> "And baby, true freedom is the open road, the wind on your face and a good woman on the back of your bike holdin’ you tight like you’re her reason for breathin’ because she sure as fuck is yours.” </i></b> <br/><br/>WARNING:<br/>This book contains...<br/><br/>*Profanities, <b> LOTS OF IT. </b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397136ra/766044.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*Violence<br/><br/>*A bunch of sexual situations, including <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ a rape scene  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/>*Infidelity<br/><br/>*and a lot more fvcked up craziness you can imagine.<br/><br/>...If you cannot handle all of that, then this book is <b> NOT </b> for you.<br/><br/>or if you think y</span>
  <span id="freeText8823300708387895687" style="display:none"><b> <i> "And baby, true freedom is the open road, the wind on your face and a good woman on the back of your bike holdin’ you tight like you’re her reason for breathin’ because she sure as fuck is yours.” </i></b> <br><br>WARNING:<br>This book contains...<br><br>*Profanities, <b> LOTS OF IT. </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397136ra/766044.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*Violence<br><br>*A bunch of sexual situations, including <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ a rape scene  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>*Infidelity<br><br>*and a lot more fvcked up craziness you can imagine.<br><br>...If you cannot handle all of that, then this book is <b> NOT </b> for you.<br><br>or if you think you do, you might need this:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397136i/766045.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> You're welcome! </i><br><br>Okay, so let me get this out of my system first.<br><br>WHAT THE ACTUAL FUCK?!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br>THIS BOOK IS CRAZY... ALL AROUND CRAZY... TANGLED WEB OF CRAZY!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397136ra/766046.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm having a difficult time creating a review for this because my emotions are all over the place. Did I really just read that?!<br><br>I just have a few issues I need to address:<br><br><b> <u> Eva </u></b>  - I just can't understand this woman. She sees Deuce, fvck him, and then you disappear. And then she marries fvcked-up-in-the-head Frankie when she can just walk away and be with the man she loves. And then when Frankie was in jail, she basically sold her soul to Chase and let him fvck her so that Frankie can go out of jail. What the hell?! <br><br>And then according to her:<br><br><b> <i> There are three different types of men in this world. There are weak men; men who run and hide when life slaps them in the ass. Then there are men; men who have a backbone yet occasionally, when life slaps them in the ass, will rely on others. And then there are real men; men who don’t cry or complain, who don’t just have a backbone, they are the backbone. Men who make their own decisions and live with the consequences, who accept responsibility for their actions or words. Men who, when life slaps them in the ass, slap back and move on.<br><br>...Men like Deuce. </i></b> <br><br>Girl, you cray cray? Deuce has NO backbone. Who in the right mind call their woman bitches? Who in the right mind lets a club whore suck his d*ck while making his woman kiss him? Who in the right mind fvcks another woman while his woman is pregnant? OH YEAH, Men like Deuce.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397136ra/766047.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So yeah, <b> <u> Deuce </u></b> <br><br>Deuce Deuce Deuce. He's such a manwhore. And often times, I just wanna kill him for fvcking other woman while Eva's pregnant and for being the reason why Eva almost dies.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397136ra/766048.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397136ra/766049.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> <u> Frankie </u></b>  - Crazy crazy messed up character. He's obssessed with Eva. I should be happy he got killed, but you know what, I kinda felt bad for him because all he ever wants is Eva. But still, he's crazy.<br><br>And all the supporting characters are fvcked up as well.<br><br>Plus, they shouldn't use profanities when they're with children. UGH.<br><br>So, how can I still give this book a high rating when all I do is complain? Well you see, that's actually the reason. You know you've read a good book when you become so attached to it. This book affected me...in a crazy fvcked up way. It made me feel. <br><br><b> <i> "Name's Deuce sweetheart. My old man<br>here is Reaper. It was nice talkin' with ya."<br>She put her tiny hand in his and he<br>squeezed.<br><br>"Eva," She whispered. "That's my name<br>and it was so, so great to meet you too."<br>He smiled.<br>She smiled.<br>The rest is fuckin’ history. </i></b> <br><br>This pretty much sums up my reading experience:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397136ra/766050.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> 4.5 UNDENIABLY FUCKED UP STARS!!! </b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12821564632416036539"><b>Just a quick re-read 7/4/17</b><br/>Get it here: <br/><a href='http://amzn.to/2tOXR1F' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a> * <a href='http://amzn.to/2sUqEgd' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a><br/><br/>Oh my god there are just no words! I absolutely loved this book, couldn't get enough of it. Deuce and Eva definitely have their issues but from the first moment they meet you know that they are meant for each other. I wasn't too sure about the age difference when I read the synopsis but when I started reading, it became a non-issue and actually added to me liking this book. Even though there were times that I wanted to smack the shit o</span>
  <span id="freeText12821564632416036539" style="display:none"><b>Just a quick re-read 7/4/17</b><br />Get it here: <br /><a href="http://amzn.to/2tOXR1F" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> * <a href="http://amzn.to/2sUqEgd" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a><br /><br />Oh my god there are just no words! I absolutely loved this book, couldn't get enough of it. Deuce and Eva definitely have their issues but from the first moment they meet you know that they are meant for each other. I wasn't too sure about the age difference when I read the synopsis but when I started reading, it became a non-issue and actually added to me liking this book. Even though there were times that I wanted to smack the shit out of Deuce I never stopped loving his character. This book was a tragic, soul crushing love story that will make you question your stand on right and wrong.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RSaKUFU0e26a538WHHkHYD1HLiFG3FPB1TrWbD4nsQw2iiJAnJhb3vY/hopGjpKtRZjElSjoBt8gAcbWYKIgnw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('W00GN25xX5P8ZPpgXhyRn02cY2hp0I9LAoL8ZTpgyUEo4a4np91/I5C8A/wE6wRSNUOJ3Afk2lX3uezfZOVY0g==')})
  }
